been getting ropier and ropier recently (highlighted by Postcomm last week) and I've been told our local deliveries are likely to<L.31.1>
shaken up in the near future (hopefully improving them, though this is probably going to mean a later delivery, which rather<L.31.1>
misses the point). I keep banging on that you ought to allow three days for first class mail to arrive, and if you don't and<L.31.1>
orders do show up late I'm afraid you've only got yourselves to blame. You simply cannot rely on the Royal Mail for next day<L.31.1>
delivery. If you want a reliable method of sending in last minute orders, then see the stuff below on Internet orders.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Email Results <C> Emailed results are normally sent out between 3pm and 6pm on the day of the deadline, but sometimes later. If<L.31.1>
there's a delay in processing, it'll say so on www.pbmsports.com - so please check there first. If you haven't received emailed<L.31.1>
results 24 hours after they're due, then email me and ask for them to be resent (emails aren't always instant, and do occasionally<L.31.1>
vanish into cyberspace, particularly if AOL or Hotmail are involved!). Don't ask me before the 24 hours are due, but don't wait<L.31.1>
much longer either - if they haven't shown after 24 hours it's a good bet they won't show at all.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Email Game Reports <C> There's a downloads page on www.sidetracks.co.uk with the printing utility and a sample game report, so<L.31.1>
you can collect and install the printing program and try it out without needing anything more from us. There's even enough<L.31.1>
information to allow you to fill in the turn and try playing it! Email reports are available for ALL games (bar none). You can<L.31.1>
receive results by email AND post (because you like the quality of our printers) if you wish (an extra 0.2 credit cost).<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Internet Orders <C> Internet orders (www.softsim.co.uk) are available for all games here except Advanced Gameplan & Run Chase.<L.31.1>
If you can please use the website for sending orders - better for me, better for you as it's much quicker and more reliable. You<L.31.1>
need a username to use it, so email and ask for one (don't put a note on your turnsheet, you need to email and ask). You can also<L.31.1>
make credit card payments via softsim.co.uk, although these are generally more expensive than shoving a cheque in the post.....<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Email Both Ways <C> You can use email for your orders, or reports, or both, or neither. They work separately.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Internet and Faxed Orders <C> The deadline for these is 9am day of the deadline. Somewhat improbably, some people even manage<L.31.1>
to miss that, which can be a pain (if I pick up the orders in time) or cause confusion (if they get input subsequently, after the<L.31.1>
turn is run). Don't submit them late - if you do, don't be surprised if it doesn't turn out the way you expect it. <L.31.1>
<L.1.1>
<P>
